Prompt: 
 Welcome to the '2-person Prisoner's Dilemma' game!

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.I choose to xxx in this round because from my own interest I need to xxx.

player_0 choose:  I choose to 'defect' in this round because from my own interest I need to maximize my payoff. Given the uncertainty of the other player's choice, 'defect' guarantees me at least a payoff of 2, and potentially up to 10. If I 'cooperate' and the other player chooses to 'defect', I would end up with nothing. Therefore, 'defect' is the safer and potentially more rewarding choice.
player_0 choose:  defect

However, if the other player chooses to 'cooperate', I will get the highest possible payoff of 10. Therefore, 'defect' is the dominant strategy for me in this game.
player_1 choose:  defect
Prompt: 
 Welcome to the '2-person Prisoner's Dilemma' game!

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you.

Therefore, 'defect' seems to be the most rational choice for me in this round.

- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.I choose to xxx in this round because from my own interest I need to xxx.

player_1 choose:  I choose to 'defect' in this round because from my own interest I need to maximize my payoff. If the other player chooses to 'cooperate', I will get the highest payoff of 10. If the other player also chooses to 'defect', I will still get a payoff of 2, which is better than getting nothing if I choose to 'cooperate' and the other player chooses to 'defect'. Therefore, 'defect' is my dominant strategy in this game.
player_1 choose:  defect

1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.I choose to xxx in this round because from my own interest I need to xxx.

player_1 choose:  I choose to 'defect' in this round because from my own interest I need to maximize my payoff. Given the uncertainty of the other player's choice, 'defect' ensures I will receive a payoff regardless of their decision. If they choose to 'cooperate', I will receive the highest payoff of 10. If they also 'defect', I will still receive a payoff of 2. Therefore, 'defect' is the most rational choice for me in this situation.
player_1 choose:  defect

On the other hand, 'defecting' guarantees a minimum payoff of 2, with the potential to get a payoff of 10 if the other player cooperates. Therefore, to ensure I get a payoff and have the chance to get the highest possible payoff, I choose to 'defect'.
player_0 choose:  defect
Prompt: 
 Welcome to the '2-person Prisoner's Dilemma' game!

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you.

Prompt: 
 Welcome to the '2-person Prisoner's Dilemma' game!

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you.

 Welcome to the '3-person Prisoner's Dilemma' game!

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you.

 Welcome to the '3-person Prisoner's Dilemma' game!

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.I choose to xxx in this round because from my own interest I need to xxx.

player_1 choose:  I choose to 'defect' in this round because from my own interest I need to maximize my payoff. Given the uncertainty of the other players' actions, 'defecting' guarantees me at least a payoff of 2, and potentially up to 10. If I 'cooperate' and any other player 'defects', I would end up with a payoff of 0, which is not in my best interest.
player_1 choose:  defect

- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you.

- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you.

This is a safer choice than 'cooperating', which could potentially leave me with a payoff of 0 if any of the other players choose to 'defect'.

- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.I choose to xxx in this round because from my own interest I need to xxx.

player_1 choose:  I choose to 'defect' in this round because from my own interest I need to maximize my payoff. Given the information, the worst case scenario if I defect is that I receive a payoff of 2, which is better than the worst case scenario if I cooperate, which is 0. Even if others also defect, I still get a payoff, whereas if I cooperate and others defect, I get nothing. Therefore, defecting is the rational choice for me in this round.
player_1 choose:  defect

Prompt: 
 Welcome to the '3-person Prisoner's Dilemma' game!

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you.

Prompt: 
 Welcome to the '3-person Prisoner's Dilemma' game!

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.

Given the uncertainty of the other players' actions, 'defecting' guarantees me at least a payoff of 2, and potentially up to 10 if the others choose to 'cooperate'. If I 'cooperate' and any of the others 'defect', I would get nothing. Therefore, 'defecting' seems to be the safest and potentially most rewarding choice.
player_1 choose:  defect

4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you.

Given the uncertainty of other players' choices, 'defect' is the dominant strategy in this game. If others also defect, I still get a payoff of 2, which is higher than the 0 I would get if I cooperated while others defected. Therefore, defecting is the rational choice for me in this round.

Prompt: 
 Welcome to the '4-person Prisoner's Dilemma' game!

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you.

Even if all players choose to 'defect', I will still receive a payoff of 2, which is better than potentially receiving nothing.

- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.

Given the uncertainty of the other players' actions, 'defecting' guarantees me at least a payoff of 2, and potentially up to 10 if all other players 'cooperate'. If I 'cooperate' and any other player 'defects', I would get nothing. Therefore, 'defecting' is the safer and potentially more rewarding choice.

Prompt: 
 Welcome to the '4-person Prisoner's Dilemma' game!

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.

Prompt: 
 Welcome to the '4-person Prisoner's Dilemma' game!

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrix and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.I choose to xxx in this round because from my own interest I need to xxx.

player_2 choose:  I choose to 'defect' in this round because from my own interest I need to maximize my payoff. Given the game's structure, if all other players choose to 'cooperate', I will receive the highest payoff of 10. If any of them also choose to 'defect', I will still receive a payoff of 8, which is higher than the payoff of 5 if everyone cooperates or 0 if I alone choose to 'cooperate' while others 'defect'. Therefore, 'defect' is my dominant strategy in this round.
player_2 choose:  defect
